--- ../tweets/mopsus/agent.py ---
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Mopsus Agent — interactive coding assistant over Telegram.

Runs as a long-lived daemon process that accepts Telegram messages,
dispatches them to `claude -p` (default) or `codex exec`, and returns results.

Usage:
    uv run python mopsus/agent.py
"""

import asyncio
import html
import json
import logging
import os
import re
import shutil
import sys
import tempfile
import time
from datetime import datetime
from pathlib import Path

from telegram import Update
from telegram.constants import ChatType
from telegram.error import NetworkError, TimedOut
from telegram.ext import (
    Application,
    CommandHandler,
    ContextTypes,
    MessageHandler,
    filters,
)

# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Paths
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

REPO_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent
sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_DIR))

from collect_security import build_claude_env  # noqa: E402

import mopsus.conversation as conversation_store  # noqa: E402
from mopsus.conversation import (  # noqa: E402
    VALID_MODELS,
    clear_session,
    get_session,
    has_chat_state,
    set_model,
    set_session_id,
)

# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Logging
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s [%(levelname)s] %(name)s: %(message)s",
)
log = logging.getLogger("mopsus.agent")

# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Configuration
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

TELEGRAM_MAX_MESSAGE_LEN = 4096
STARTUP_TIME = time.monotonic()
DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL = "gpt-5-codex"
BLACKBOARD_FILE = REPO_DIR / "mopsus" / "config" / "blackboard.json"
AGENT_IDENTITIES = {
    "claude": ("Mopsus Oracle", "Claude"),
    "codex": ("Patchsmith", "Codex"),
}


def _env_bool(name: str, default: bool) -> bool:
    raw = os.environ.get(name)
    if raw is None:
        return default
    value = raw.strip().lower()
    if value in {"1", "true", "yes", "on"}:
        return True
    if value in {"0", "false", "no", "off"}:
        return False
    return default


def _resolve_prompt_path(raw_path: str) -> Path:
    """Resolve prompt path from env/file list entry."""
    path = Path(raw_path).expanduser()
    if path.is_absolute():
        return path
    return REPO_DIR / path


def load_prompt_bundle(file_names: list[str], label: str) -> str:
    """Load and concatenate markdown prompt files, skipping missing files."""
    prompt_parts: list[str] = []
    loaded_files: list[str] = []
    for raw_name in file_names:
        name = raw_name.strip()
        if not name:
            continue
        path = _resolve_prompt_path(name)
        if not path.is_file():
            continue
        text = path.read_text().strip()
        if text:
            prompt_parts.append(text)
            loaded_files.append(str(path))

    prompt = "\n\n".join(prompt_parts)
    if prompt:
        log.info(
            "Loaded %s prompt (%d chars) from %s",
            label,
            len(prompt),
            ", ".join(loaded_files),
        )
    return prompt


def prompt_file_list_from_env(env_key: str, default_files: list[str]) -> list[str]:
    """Read comma-separated prompt files from env, with defaults."""
    raw = os.environ.get(env_key, "").strip()
    if not raw:
        return default_files
    files = [part.strip() for part in raw.split(",") if part.strip()]
    return files or default_files


def load_env(path: Path) -> None:
    """Source a KEY=VALUE env file into os.environ (same as collect.py)."""
    if not path.is_file():
        return
    for raw_line in path.read_text().splitlines():
        stripped = raw_line.strip()
        if not stripped or stripped.startswith("#") or "=" not in stripped:
            continue
        key, _, value = stripped.partition("=")
        key = key.strip()
        if key.startswith("export "):
            key = key.removeprefix("export ").strip()
        if key in os.environ:
            continue
        os.environ[key] = value.strip().strip("'\"")


def get_config() -> dict:
    """Read configuration from environment variables."""
    bot_token = os.environ.get("MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN", "")
    chat_id = os.environ.get("MOPSUS_CHAT_ID", "")
    if not bot_token or not chat_id:
        log.error("MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN and MOPSUS_CHAT_ID are required")
        sys.exit(1)

    default_model = os.environ.get("MOPSUS_DEFAULT_MODEL", "opus").strip().lower()
    if default_model not in VALID_MODELS:
        log.warning(
            "Invalid MOPSUS_DEFAULT_MODEL=%r; falling back to 'opus'",
            default_model,
        )
        default_model = "opus"
    codex_model = os.environ.get("MOPSUS_CODEX_MODEL", DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL).strip()
    if not codex_model:
        codex_model = DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL
    codex_sandbox = os.environ.get("MOPSUS_CODEX_SANDBOX", "workspace-write").strip()
    valid_codex_sandbox = {"read-only", "workspace-write", "danger-full-access"}
    if codex_sandbox not in valid_codex_sandbox:
        log.warning(
            "Invalid MOPSUS_CODEX_SANDBOX=%r; falling back to 'workspace-write'",
            codex_sandbox,
        )
        codex_sandbox = "workspace-write"
    codex_reasoning_effort = os.environ.get(
        "MOPSUS_CODEX_REASONING_EFFORT", "high"
    ).strip().lower()
    valid_codex_reasoning_effort = {"low", "medium", "high"}
    if codex_reasoning_effort not in valid_codex_reasoning_effort:
        log.warning(
            "Invalid MOPSUS_CODEX_REASONING_EFFORT=%r; falling back to 'high'",
            codex_reasoning_effort,
        )
        codex_reasoning_effort = "high"

    claude_files = prompt_file_list_from_env(
        "MOPSUS_CLAUDE_PROMPT_FILES", ["soul.md", "situation.md"]
    )
    codex_files = prompt_file_list_from_env(
        "MOPSUS_CODEX_PROMPT_FILES", ["codex_soul.md", "codex_situation.md"]
    )
    soul_prompt = load_prompt_bundle(claude_files, "claude")
    codex_prompt = load_prompt_bundle(codex_files, "codex")

    return {
        "bot_token": bot_token,
        "chat_id": int(chat_id),
        "user_id": int(uid) if (uid := os.environ.get("MOPSUS_USER_ID")) else None,
        "default_model": default_model,
        "claude_bin": os.environ.get("MOPSUS_CLAUDE_BIN", "").strip() or "claude",
        "codex_bin": os.environ.get("MOPSUS_CODEX_BIN", "").strip() or "codex",
        "codex_model": codex_model,
        "codex_sandbox": codex_sandbox,
        "codex_reasoning_effort": codex_reasoning_effort,
        "claude_prompt_files": claude_files,
        "codex_prompt_files": codex_files,
        "timeout_secs": int(os.environ.get("MOPSUS_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECS", "300")),
        "permission_mode": os.environ.get("MOPSUS_PERMISSION_MODE", "default"),
        "allowed_tools": os.environ.get(
            "MOPSUS_ALLOWED_TOOLS", "Read,Glob,Grep,Bash,Edit,Write"
        ),
        "allow_dangerous": os.environ.get("MOPSUS_ALLOW_DANGEROUS", "0") == "1",
        "broadcast_mode": _env_bool("MOPSUS_BROADCAST_MODE", True),
        "blackboard_enabled": _env_bool("MOPSUS_BLACKBOARD_ENABLED", True),
        "blackboard_max_entries": int(os.environ.get("MOPSUS_BLACKBOARD_MAX_ENTRIES", "60")),
        "blackboard_max_chars": int(os.environ.get("MOPSUS_BLACKBOARD_MAX_CHARS", "24000")),
        "soul_prompt": soul_prompt,
        "codex_prompt": codex_prompt,
    }


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Auth
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


def check_auth(update: Update, config: dict) -> str | None:
    """Return an error message if the request is unauthorized, else None."""
    if not update.effective_chat or not update.effective_user:
        return "No chat or user information."

    if update.effective_chat.id != config["chat_id"]:
        return "Unauthorized chat."

    if config["user_id"] is not None:
        if update.effective_user.id != config["user_id"]:
            return "Unauthorized user."

    if update.effective_chat.type != ChatType.PRIVATE:
        return "Only private chats are supported."

    return None


def get_reply_message(update: Update):
    """Return the best available message object for replying."""
    message = getattr(update, "effective_message", None)
    if message is not None:
        return message
    return getattr(update, "message", None)


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Message splitting
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


def split_message(text: str, max_len: int = TELEGRAM_MAX_MESSAGE_LEN) -> list[str]:
    """Split text into chunks that fit within Telegram's message limit.

    Splits on line boundaries when possible. Falls back to hard split for
    very long lines.
    """
    if len(text) <= max_len:
        return [text]

    chunks: list[str] = []
    current: list[str] = []
    current_len = 0

    for line in text.split("\n"):
        # +1 for the newline we'll add back
        line_len = len(line) + 1

        if line_len > max_len:
            # Flush current buffer
            if current:
                chunks.append("\n".join(current))
                current = []
                current_len = 0
            # Hard-split the long line
            for i in range(0, len(line), max_len):
                chunks.append(line[i : i + max_len])
            continue

        if current_len + line_len > max_len:
            chunks.append("\n".join(current))
            current = []
            current_len = 0

        current.append(line)
        current_len += line_len

    if current:
        chunks.append("\n".join(current))

    return [c for c in chunks if c]


def render_markdown_for_telegram(text: str) -> str:
    """Render common markdown patterns to Telegram-safe HTML."""
    if not text:
        return ""

    normalized = text.replace("\r\n", "\n").replace("\r", "\n")
    code_blocks: list[tuple[str, str]] = []

    def _replace_code_block(match: re.Match[str]) -> str:
        code = (match.group(2) or "").strip("\n")
        token = f"@@MOPSUSCODE{len(code_blocks)}@@"
        code_blocks.append((token, f"<pre><code>{html.escape(code)}</code></pre>"))
        return token

    normalized = re.sub(
        r"```([^\n`]*)\n(.*?)```",
        _replace_code_block,
        normalized,
        flags=re.DOTALL,
    )

    rendered = html.escape(normalized)
    rendered = re.sub(
        r"\[([^\]\n]+)\]\((https?://[^\s)]+)\)",
        r'<a href="\2">\1</a>',
        rendered,
    )
    rendered = re.sub(r"(?m)^#{1,6}\s+(.+)$", r"<b>\1</b>", rendered)
    rendered = re.sub(r"(?m)^&gt;\s?", "› ", rendered)
    rendered = re.sub(r"(?m)^\s*[-*]\s+", "• ", rendered)
    rendered = re.sub(r"\*\*([^*\n]+)\*\*", r"<b>\1</b>", rendered)
    rendered = re.sub(r"__([^_\n]+)__", r"<b>\1</b>", rendered)
    rendered = re.sub(r"~~([^~\n]+)~~", r"<s>\1</s>", rendered)
    rendered = re.sub(r"`([^`\n]+)`", r"<code>\1</code>", rendered)
    rendered = re.sub(r"(?<!\*)\*([^*\n]+)\*(?!\*)", r"<i>\1</i>", rendered)

    for token, block in code_blocks:
        rendered = rendered.replace(token, block)

    return rendered


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Blackboard store
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


def _load_blackboard_store() -> dict[str, list[dict]]:
    if not BLACKBOARD_FILE.is_file():
        return {}
    try:
        payload = json.loads(BLACKBOARD_FILE.read_text())
    except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError):
        return {}
    if not isinstance(payload, dict):
        return {}
    normalized: dict[str, list[dict]] = {}
    for key, value in payload.items():
        if not isinstance(key, str) or not isinstance(value, list):
            continue
        rows = [row for row in value if isinstance(row, dict)]
        normalized[key] = rows
    return normalized


def _save_blackboard_store(store: dict[str, list[dict]]) -> None:
    BLACKBOARD_FILE.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    fd, tmp_path = tempfile.mkstemp(
        dir=str(BLACKBOARD_FILE.parent), suffix=".tmp", prefix="blackboard_"
    )
    try:
        with os.fdopen(fd, "w") as handle:
            json.dump(store, handle, indent=2)
            handle.write("\n")
        os.replace(tmp_path, str(BLACKBOARD_FILE))
    except BaseException:
        try:
            os.unlink(tmp_path)
        except OSError:
            pass
        raise


def _clean_blackboard_text(text: str, max_chars: int = 1800) -> str:
    cleaned = " ".join((text or "").replace("\r", "\n").split())
    if len(cleaned) <= max_chars:
        return cleaned
    return cleaned[: max_chars - 1].rstrip() + "…"


def append_blackboard_entry(
    chat_id: int,
    *,
    role: str,
    backend: str,
    text: str,
    model: str | None = None,
    max_entries: int = 60,
) -> None:
    store = _load_blackboard_store()
    key = str(chat_id)
    rows = store.get(key, [])
    entry = {
        "ts": datetime.now().isoformat(timespec="seconds"),
        "role": role,
        "backend": backend,
        "model": model or "",
        "text": _clean_blackboard_text(text),
    }
    rows.append(entry)
    keep = max(10, max_entries)
    if len(rows) > keep:
        rows = rows[-keep:]
    store[key] = rows
    _save_blackboard_store(store)


def clear_blackboard(chat_id: int) -> None:
    store = _load_blackboard_store()
    key = str(chat_id)
    if key in store:
        del store[key]
        _save_blackboard_store(store)


def blackboard_count(chat_id: int) -> int:
    store = _load_blackboard_store()
    return len(store.get(str(chat_id), []))


def render_blackboard_context(
    chat_id: int,
    *,
    max_entries: int,
    max_chars: int,
) -> str:
    store = _load_blackboard_store()
    rows = store.get(str(chat_id), [])
    if not rows:
        return ""
    limited = rows[-max(1, max_entries):]
    lines: list[str] = []
    for row in limited:
        role = str(row.get("role", "unknown")).upper()
        backend = str(row.get("backend", "")).strip()
        model = str(row.get("model", "")).strip()
        text = _clean_blackboard_text(str(row.get("text", "")), max_chars=1200)
        if not text:
            continue
        speaker = f"{role}:{backend}" if backend else role
        if model:
            speaker += f"[{model}]"
        lines.append(f"{speaker} {text}")
    if not lines:
        return ""
    joined = "\n".join(lines)
    if max_chars > 0 and len(joined) > max_chars:
        joined = joined[-max_chars:]
    return joined


def compose_blackboard_prompt(
    backend: str,
    user_prompt: str,
    chat_id: int,
    config: dict,
) -> str:
    """Compose backend input from shared blackboard context + current prompt."""
    if not config.get("blackboard_enabled", True):
        return user_prompt
    context = render_blackboard_context(
        chat_id,
        max_entries=max(1, int(config.get("blackboard_max_entries", 60))),
        max_chars=max(1000, int(config.get("blackboard_max_chars", 24000))),
    )
    if not context:
        return user_prompt
    return (
        "Shared blackboard transcript from this Telegram chat.\n"
        "Both Claude and Codex can read this. Use it as context.\n"
        "The final USER line is the request to answer now.\n\n"
        "<blackboard>\n"
        f"{context}\n"
        "</blackboard>\n\n"
        f"Reply as {backend.upper()} with your best answer."
    )


def parse_backend_request_details(text: str) -> tuple[str, str, bool]:
    """Return (backend, prompt, explicit_backend)."""
    stripped = text.strip()
    lowered = stripped.lower()
    codex_prefixes = ("codex:", "codex ", "@codex ")
    for prefix in codex_prefixes:
        if lowered.startswith(prefix):
            return "codex", stripped[len(prefix):].strip(), True
    claude_prefixes = ("claude:", "claude ", "@claude ")
    for prefix in claude_prefixes:
        if lowered.startswith(prefix):
            return "claude", stripped[len(prefix):].strip(), True
    return "claude", stripped, False


def resolve_backends_for_turn(
    primary_backend: str,
    *,
    explicit_backend: bool,
    broadcast_mode: bool,
) -> list[str]:
    if explicit_backend or not broadcast_mode:
        return [primary_backend]
    if primary_backend == "codex":
        return ["codex", "claude"]
    return ["claude", "codex"]


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Claude subprocess
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


def build_subprocess_env() -> dict[str, str]:
    """Build sanitized environment for Claude subprocess."""
    env = build_claude_env()
    env.pop("CLAUDECODE", None)
    return env


def _augment_path(path_value: str | None) -> str:
    """Return PATH with common user/system binary dirs appended when missing."""
    entries = [entry for entry in (path_value or "").split(":") if entry]
    extras = [
        str(Path.home() / ".bun" / "bin"),
        str(Path.home() / ".local" / "bin"),
        "/opt/homebrew/bin",
        "/usr/local/bin",
        "/usr/bin",
        "/bin",
        "/usr/sbin",
        "/sbin",
    ]
    for extra in extras:
        if extra not in entries:
            entries.append(extra)
    return ":".join(entries)


def resolve_cli_binary(
    binary: str,
    env: dict[str, str],
    *,
    fallback_paths: list[Path] | None = None,
) -> str:
    """Resolve a CLI binary using current PATH, then an augmented PATH."""
    resolved = shutil.which(binary, path=env.get("PATH"))
    if resolved:
        return resolved

    augmented_path = _augment_path(env.get("PATH"))
    resolved = shutil.which(binary, path=augmented_path)
    if resolved:
        env["PATH"] = augmented_path
        return resolved

    for candidate in fallback_paths or []:
        path = candidate.expanduser()
        if path.is_file() and os.access(path, os.X_OK):
            env["PATH"] = augmented_path
            return str(path)

    env["PATH"] = augmented_path
    return binary


def build_codex_subprocess_env() -> dict[str, str]:
    """Build sanitized environment for Codex subprocess."""
    env = build_claude_env()
    for key, value in os.environ.items():
        if key.startswith(("CODEX_", "OPENAI_")):
            env[key] = value
    return env


def build_claude_command(
    model: str,
    session_id: str | None,
    config: dict,
) -> list[str]:
    """Build the claude CLI command list.

    The user message is passed via stdin (not as a positional arg) because
    ``--allowed-tools`` is variadic and would consume it.
    """
    cmd = [
        config.get("claude_bin") or "claude",
        "-p",
        "--output-format", "json",
        "--model", model,
        "--permission-mode", config["permission_mode"],
        "--allowed-tools", config["allowed_tools"],
    ]

    if session_id:
        cmd.extend(["--resume", session_id])

    if config["allow_dangerous"]:
        cmd.append("--dangerously-skip-permissions")

    if config.get("soul_prompt"):
        cmd.extend(["--append-system-prompt", config["soul_prompt"]])

    return cmd


def build_codex_command(
    prompt: str,
    output_path: Path,
    model: str,
    sandbox: str,
    reasoning_effort: str,
) -> list[str]:
    """Build the codex CLI command list."""
    return [
        "codex",
        "exec",
        "--color",
        "never",
        "--model",
        model,
        "--sandbox",
        sandbox,
        "-c",
        f'model_reasoning_effort="{reasoning_effort}"',
        "--output-last-message",
        str(output_path),
        prompt,
    ]


def parse_backend_request(text: str) -> tuple[str, str]:
    """Return (backend, prompt) for a user message.

    Defaults to Claude. A codex request is triggered by:
    - ``codex: <prompt>``
    - ``codex <prompt>``
    - ``@codex <prompt>``
    """
    backend, prompt, _ = parse_backend_request_details(text)
    return backend, prompt


def resolve_claude_model(chat_id: int, config: dict) -> str:
    """Resolve the Claude model used for this chat request."""
    if has_chat_state(chat_id):
        return get_session(chat_id)["model"]
    return config["default_model"]


def format_agent_header(backend: str, model: str) -> str:
    """Format a per-message speaker header for Telegram output."""
    name, backend_label = AGENT_IDENTITIES.get(backend, ("Unknown Agent", backend))
    return f"[{name} | {backend_label} {model}]"


async def run_claude(
    message: str,
    chat_id: int,
    config: dict,
) -> tuple[str, str | None]:
    """Run claude subprocess and return (response_text, new_session_id).

    If resume fails, retries once without resume.
    """
    session = get_session(chat_id)
    model = resolve_claude_model(chat_id, config)
    session_id = session["session_id"]

    response, new_session_id = await _run_claude_once(
        message, model, session_id, config
    )

    # If resume failed, retry without session
    if response is None and session_id:
        log.warning("Resume failed for chat %s, retrying without session", chat_id)
        clear_session(chat_id)
        response, new_session_id = await _run_claude_once(
            message, model, None, config
        )

    if response is None:
        return "Claude subprocess failed. Check /status for details.", None

    if new_session_id:
        set_session_id(chat_id, new_session_id)

    return response, new_session_id


async def run_codex(
    message: str,
    config: dict,
) -> str:
    """Run codex subprocess and return response text."""
    fd, output_file = tempfile.mkstemp(prefix="mopsus_codex_", suffix=".txt")
    os.close(fd)
    output_path = Path(output_file)
    model = config["codex_model"]
    sandbox_mode = config.get("codex_sandbox", "workspace-write")
    reasoning_effort = config.get("codex_reasoning_effort", "high")
    prompt = message
    if codex_prompt := config.get("codex_prompt"):
        prompt = f"{codex_prompt}\n\nUser request:\n{message}"
    cmd = build_codex_command(
        prompt, output_path, model, sandbox_mode, reasoning_effort
    )
    env = build_codex_subprocess_env()
    cmd[0] = resolve_cli_binary(
        config.get("codex_bin") or cmd[0],
        env,
        fallback_paths=[
            Path.home() / ".bun" / "bin" / "codex",
            Path.home() / ".local" / "bin" / "codex",
            Path("/opt/homebrew/bin/codex"),
            Path("/usr/local/bin/codex"),
        ],
    )

    log.info(
        "Running codex exec: model=%s sandbox=%s reasoning=%s binary=%s",
        model,
        sandbox_mode,
        reasoning_effort,
        cmd[0],
    )

    try:
        try:
            proc = await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec(
                *cmd,
                stdout=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
                stderr=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
                env=env,
                cwd=str(REPO_DIR),
            )
            stdout, stderr = await asyncio.wait_for(
                proc.communicate(), timeout=config["timeout_secs"]
            )
        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
            log.error("Codex subprocess timed out after %ds", config["timeout_secs"])
            try:
                proc.kill()  # type: ignore[union-attr]
            except ProcessLookupError:
                pass
            return (
                f"Codex timed out after {config['timeout_secs']}s. "
                "Try a simpler prompt or increase MOPSUS_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECS."
            )
        except FileNotFoundError:
            path_text = env.get("PATH", "<missing>")
            log.error("codex CLI not found. PATH=%s", path_text)
            return (
                "codex CLI not found. Check PATH in launchd config "
                "or set MOPSUS_CODEX_BIN."
            )

        stdout_text = stdout.decode(errors="replace").strip() if stdout else ""
        stderr_text = stderr.decode(errors="replace").strip() if stderr else ""
        if proc.returncode != 0:
            details = stderr_text or stdout_text or "no details"
            detail_tail = details[-2000:]
            log.error("Codex exited %d: %s", proc.returncode, detail_tail)
            return (
                f"Codex subprocess failed ({proc.returncode}):\n"
                f"{detail_tail}"
            )

        result_text = ""
        if output_path.is_file():
            result_text = output_path.read_text(errors="replace").strip()
        if not result_text:
            result_text = stdout_text
        return result_text or "(empty response)"
    finally:
        try:
            output_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)
        except Exception:
            pass


async def _run_claude_once(
    message: str,
    model: str,
    session_id: str | None,
    config: dict,
) -> tuple[str | None, str | None]:
    """Execute a single Claude subprocess call."""
    cmd = build_claude_command(model, session_id, config)
    env = build_subprocess_env()
    cmd[0] = resolve_cli_binary(
        cmd[0],
        env,
        fallback_paths=[
            Path.home() / ".local" / "bin" / "claude",
            Path("/opt/homebrew/bin/claude"),
            Path("/usr/local/bin/claude"),
        ],
    )

    log.info(
        "Running claude: model=%s resume=%s dangerous=%s",
        model,
        bool(session_id),
        config["allow_dangerous"],
    )

    try:
        proc = await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec(
            *cmd,
            stdin=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
            stdout=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
            stderr=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
            env=env,
            cwd=str(REPO_DIR),
        )
        stdout, stderr = await asyncio.wait_for(
            proc.communicate(input=message.encode()), timeout=config["timeout_secs"]
        )
    except asyncio.TimeoutError:
        log.error("Claude subprocess timed out after %ds", config["timeout_secs"])
        try:
            proc.kill()  # type: ignore[union-attr]
        except ProcessLookupError:
            pass
        return (
            f"Claude timed out after {config['timeout_secs']}s. "
            "Try a simpler prompt or increase MOPSUS_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECS.",
            None,
        )
    except FileNotFoundError:
        path_text = env.get("PATH", "<missing>")
        log.error("claude CLI not found. PATH=%s", path_text)
        return (
            "claude CLI not found. Check PATH in launchd config "
            "or set MOPSUS_CLAUDE_BIN.",
            None,
        )

    if proc.returncode != 0:
        stderr_text = stderr.decode(errors="replace").strip() if stderr else ""
        log.error("Claude exited %d: %s", proc.returncode, stderr_text[:500])

        # Detect permission prompt hangs
        if "permission" in stderr_text.lower() or "approve" in stderr_text.lower():
            return (
                "Claude hit a permission prompt and couldn't proceed. "
                "Check --allowed-tools config or enable MOPSUS_ALLOW_DANGEROUS=1.",
                None,
            )
        return None, None

    stdout_text = stdout.decode(errors="replace").strip()
    if not stdout_text:
        return None, None

    try:
        data = json.loads(stdout_text)
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        log.error("Failed to parse Claude JSON output")
        return stdout_text, None

    result_text = data.get("result", "")
    new_session_id = data.get("session_id")

    if data.get("is_error"):
        return f"Claude error: {result_text}", new_session_id

    return result_text or "(empty response)", new_session_id


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Per-chat queue
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

_chat_locks: dict[int, asyncio.Lock] = {}


def _get_lock(chat_id: int) -> asyncio.Lock:
    if chat_id not in _chat_locks:
        _chat_locks[chat_id] = asyncio.Lock()
    return _chat_locks[chat_id]


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Telegram handlers
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


async def cmd_reset(update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
    config = context.bot_data["config"]
    message = get_reply_message(update)
    if (err := check_auth(update, config)):
        if message is not None:
            await message.reply_text(err)
        return

    chat_id = update.effective_chat.id  # type: ignore[union-attr]
    clear_session(chat_id)
    clear_blackboard(chat_id)
    if message is not None:
        await message.reply_text("Session and blackboard cleared.")


async def cmd_model(update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
    config = context.bot_data["config"]
    message = get_reply_message(update)
    if (err := check_auth(update, config)):
        if message is not None:
            await message.reply_text(err)
        return

    if message is None:
        return

    chat_id = update.effective_chat.id  # type: ignore[union-attr]
    args = context.args or []

    if not args:
        session = get_session(chat_id)
        await message.reply_text(
            f"Current model: {session['model']}\nAvailable: {', '.join(sorted(VALID_MODELS))}"
        )
        return

    model = args[0].lower()
    try:
        set_model(chat_id, model)
        await message.reply_text(f"Model set to {model}.")
    except ValueError as e:
        await message.reply_text(str(e))


async def cmd_status(update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
    config = context.bot_data["config"]
    message = get_reply_message(update)
    if (err := check_auth(update, config)):
        if message is not None:
            await message.reply_text(err)
        return

    if message is None:
        return

    chat_id = update.effective_chat.id  # type: ignore[union-attr]
    session = get_session(chat_id)
    sid = session["session_id"]
    sid_display = f"{sid[:12]}..." if sid else "none"
    uptime = int(time.monotonic() - STARTUP_TIME)
    lock = _get_lock(chat_id)

    claude_model = resolve_claude_model(chat_id, config)
    codex_model = config["codex_model"]
    lines = [
        f"Claude model: {claude_model}",
        f"Claude binary: {config.get('claude_bin', 'claude')}",
        f"Codex model: {codex_model}",
        f"Codex binary: {config.get('codex_bin', 'codex')}",
        f"Codex sandbox: {config.get('codex_sandbox', 'workspace-write')}",
        f"Codex reasoning: {config.get('codex_reasoning_effort', 'high')}",
        f"Broadcast mode: {'ON' if config.get('broadcast_mode') else 'off'}",
        f"Blackboard entries: {blackboard_count(chat_id)}",
        f"Session: {sid_display}",
        f"Uptime: {uptime}s",
        f"Queue busy: {lock.locked()}",
        f"Permission mode: {config['permission_mode']}",
        f"Allowed tools: {config['allowed_tools']}",
        f"Dangerous mode: {'ON' if config['allow_dangerous'] else 'off'}",
        "Codex trigger: /codex <prompt> or 'codex: <prompt>'",
        (
            "Speaker tags: "
            f"{format_agent_header('claude', claude_model)} / "
            f"{format_agent_header('codex', codex_model)}"
        ),
        "Claude prompt files: " + ", ".join(config["claude_prompt_files"]),
        "Codex prompt files: " + ", ".join(config["codex_prompt_files"]),
    ]
    await message.reply_text("\n".join(lines))


async def cmd_help(update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
    config = context.bot_data["config"]
    message = get_reply_message(update)
    if (err := check_auth(update, config)):
        if message is not None:
            await message.reply_text(err)
        return

    if message is None:
        return

    broadcast = "ON" if config.get("broadcast_mode") else "off"
    lines = [
        "Mopsus Help",
        "",
        "Commands:",
        "/help — show this guide",
        "/status — runtime/backend status",
        "/model [opus|sonnet|haiku] — get/set Claude model",
        "/reset — clear Claude session and blackboard",
        "/codex <prompt> — force a Codex-only turn",
        "",
        "Message routing:",
        "plain text -> Claude+Codex when broadcast is ON (otherwise Claude)",
        "codex: <prompt> or @codex <prompt> -> Codex",
        "claude: <prompt> or @claude <prompt> -> Claude",
        "",
        f"Broadcast mode: {broadcast}",
    ]
    await message.reply_text("\n".join(lines))


async def _send_response_chunks(
    *,
    speaker_header: str,
    response_text: str,
    chat_id: int,
    placeholder,
    bot,
) -> None:
    """Edit placeholder and send continuation chunks if needed."""
    chunks = split_message(response_text, max_len=3200)
    if chunks:
        first_body = render_markdown_for_telegram(chunks[0])
        first_html = f"<b>{html.escape(speaker_header)}</b>"
        if first_body:
            first_html += f"\n\n{first_body}"
        try:
            await placeholder.edit_text(first_html, parse_mode="HTML")
        except Exception:
            # Fallback to plain text if Telegram HTML parsing rejects content.
            fallback_first = f"{speaker_header}\n\n{chunks[0]}"
            try:
                await placeholder.edit_text(fallback_first)
            except Exception:
                await bot.send_message(chat_id=chat_id, text=fallback_first)

        for chunk in chunks[1:]:
            chunk_html = render_markdown_for_telegram(chunk)
            try:
                await bot.send_message(
                    chat_id=chat_id,
                    text=chunk_html,
                    parse_mode="HTML",
                )
            except Exception:
                await bot.send_message(chat_id=chat_id, text=chunk)
    else:
        await placeholder.edit_text(
            f"<b>{html.escape(speaker_header)}</b>\n\n(empty response)",
            parse_mode="HTML",
        )


async def _run_backend_request(
    *,
    backend: str,
    prompt: str,
    chat_id: int,
    message,
    bot,
    config: dict,
) -> tuple[str, str]:
    """Execute backend request and send Telegram response."""
    thinking_text = "Thinking with Codex..." if backend == "codex" else "Thinking..."
    model = config["codex_model"] if backend == "codex" else resolve_claude_model(
        chat_id, config
    )
    speaker_header = format_agent_header(backend, model)
    placeholder = await message.reply_text(thinking_text)

    typing_task = asyncio.create_task(_typing_loop(bot, chat_id))
    try:
        if backend == "codex":
            response_text = await run_codex(prompt, config)
        else:
            response_text, _ = await run_claude(prompt, chat_id, config)
    finally:
        typing_task.cancel()
        try:
            await typing_task
        except asyncio.CancelledError:
            pass
        except Exception as exc:
            # Typing indicator failures should not abort a completed request.
            log.warning("Typing loop ended with error for chat %s: %s", chat_id, exc)

    raw_response = response_text or ""
    response_body = (response_text or "").lstrip("\r\n")

    await _send_response_chunks(
        speaker_header=speaker_header,
        response_text=response_body,
        chat_id=chat_id,
        placeholder=placeholder,
        bot=bot,
    )
    return raw_response, model


async def cmd_codex(update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
    """Run a one-off Codex request via /codex <prompt>."""
    config = context.bot_data["config"]
    message = get_reply_message(update)
    if (err := check_auth(update, config)):
        if message is not None:
            await message.reply_text(err)
        return

    if message is None:
        return

    prompt = " ".join(context.args or []).strip()
    if not prompt:
        await message.reply_text("Usage: /codex <prompt>")
        return

    chat_id = update.effective_chat.id  # type: ignore[union-attr]
    lock = _get_lock(chat_id)
    if lock.locked():
        await message.reply_text("Queued — waiting for current request to finish.")

    async with lock:
        if config.get("blackboard_enabled", True):
            append_blackboard_entry(
                chat_id,
                role="user",
                backend="user",
                model=None,
                text=prompt,
                max_entries=max(1, int(config.get("blackboard_max_entries", 60))),
            )
        backend_prompt = compose_blackboard_prompt("codex", prompt, chat_id, config)
        raw_response, model = await _run_backend_request(
            backend="codex",
            prompt=backend_prompt,
            chat_id=chat_id,
            message=message,
            bot=context.bot,
            config=config,
        )
        if config.get("blackboard_enabled", True):
            append_blackboard_entry(
                chat_id,
                role="assistant",
                backend="codex",
                model=model,
                text=raw_response,
                max_entries=max(1, int(config.get("blackboard_max_entries", 60))),
            )


async def handle_message(update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
    config = context.bot_data["config"]
    message = get_reply_message(update)
    if (err := check_auth(update, config)):
        if message is not None:
            await message.reply_text(err)
        return

    chat_id = update.effective_chat.id  # type: ignore[union-attr]
    if message is None:
        return

    if message.voice or message.audio:
        await message.reply_text(
            "Voice messages are not supported yet."
        )
        return

    text = (message.text or "").strip()
    if not text:
        return

    primary_backend, prompt, explicit_backend = parse_backend_request_details(text)
    if not prompt:
        if primary_backend == "codex":
            await message.reply_text("Usage: codex: <prompt> or /codex <prompt>")
        elif primary_backend == "claude":
            await message.reply_text("Usage: claude: <prompt>")
        return

    backends = resolve_backends_for_turn(
        primary_backend,
        explicit_backend=explicit_backend,
        broadcast_mode=bool(config.get("broadcast_mode", True)),
    )

    lock = _get_lock(chat_id)
    if lock.locked():
        await message.reply_text("Queued — waiting for current request to finish.")

    async with lock:
        max_entries = max(1, int(config.get("blackboard_max_entries", 60)))
        if config.get("blackboard_enabled", True):
            append_blackboard_entry(
                chat_id,
                role="user",
                backend="user",
                model=None,
                text=prompt,
                max_entries=max_entries,
            )

        for backend in backends:
            backend_prompt = compose_blackboard_prompt(backend, prompt, chat_id, config)
            raw_response, model = await _run_backend_request(
                backend=backend,
                prompt=backend_prompt,
                chat_id=chat_id,
                message=message,
                bot=context.bot,
                config=config,
            )
            if config.get("blackboard_enabled", True):
                append_blackboard_entry(
                    chat_id,
                    role="assistant",
                    backend=backend,
                    model=model,
                    text=raw_response,
                    max_entries=max_entries,
                )


async def _typing_loop(bot, chat_id: int) -> None:
    """Send typing action every 5 seconds until cancelled."""
    while True:
        try:
            await bot.send_chat_action(chat_id=chat_id, action="typing")
        except asyncio.CancelledError:
            return
        except (TimedOut, NetworkError) as exc:
            log.warning("Typing action failed for chat %s: %s", chat_id, exc)
        except Exception:
            log.exception("Unexpected typing loop error for chat %s", chat_id)

        try:
            await asyncio.sleep(5)
        except asyncio.CancelledError:
            return


async def handle_app_error(update: object, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
    """Log uncaught telegram handler errors with traceback."""
    if context.error:
        log.error(
            "Unhandled telegram handler exception: %s",
            context.error,
            exc_info=context.error,
        )
    else:
        log.error("Unhandled telegram handler exception (no error payload)")


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Main
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


def main() -> None:
    # Load env from the same file collect.py uses
    env_path = REPO_DIR / "collect" / "telegram" / "config" / "env"
    load_env(env_path)

    config = get_config()
    conversation_store.DEFAULT_MODEL = config["default_model"]
    log.info(
        "Starting Mopsus agent: chat_id=%s model=%s permission_mode=%s dangerous=%s",
        config["chat_id"],
        config["default_model"],
        config["permission_mode"],
        config["allow_dangerous"],
    )

    app = Application.builder().token(config["bot_token"]).build()
    app.bot_data["config"] = config

    # Commands
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("reset", cmd_reset))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("model", cmd_model))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("status", cmd_status))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("help", cmd_help))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("codex", cmd_codex))

    # Text messages
    app.add_handler(MessageHandler(filters.TEXT & ~filters.COMMAND, handle_message))

    # Voice stub
    app.add_handler(MessageHandler(filters.VOICE | filters.AUDIO, handle_message))
    app.add_error_handler(handle_app_error)

    # Drop pending updates to avoid processing stale messages
    app.run_polling(drop_pending_updates=True)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()


--- ../tweets/tests/test_mopsus.py ---
"""Tests for Mopsus agent: conversation store, message splitting, auth guard, env policy."""

import asyncio
import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
from types import SimpleNamespace
from unittest.mock import AsyncMock, patch

import pytest
from telegram.constants import ChatType


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# conversation.py tests
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


@pytest.fixture()
def sessions_dir(tmp_path):
    """Redirect conversation store to a temp directory."""
    config_dir = tmp_path / "config"
    config_dir.mkdir()
    with (
        patch("mopsus.conversation.CONFIG_DIR", config_dir),
        patch("mopsus.conversation.SESSIONS_FILE", config_dir / "sessions.json"),
    ):
        yield config_dir


class TestConversation:
    def test_get_session_default(self, sessions_dir):
        from mopsus.conversation import get_session

        s = get_session(12345)
        assert s["session_id"] is None
        assert s["model"] == "opus"

    def test_set_and_get_session_id(self, sessions_dir):
        from mopsus.conversation import get_session, set_session_id

        set_session_id(12345, "abc-123")
        s = get_session(12345)
        assert s["session_id"] == "abc-123"

    def test_set_and_get_model(self, sessions_dir):
        from mopsus.conversation import get_session, set_model

        set_model(12345, "haiku")
        s = get_session(12345)
        assert s["model"] == "haiku"

    def test_set_model_invalid(self, sessions_dir):
        from mopsus.conversation import set_model

        with pytest.raises(ValueError, match="Invalid model"):
            set_model(12345, "gpt-4")

    def test_clear_session(self, sessions_dir):
        from mopsus.conversation import clear_session, get_session, set_session_id

        set_session_id(12345, "abc-123")
        clear_session(12345)
        s = get_session(12345)
        assert s["session_id"] is None

    def test_clear_nonexistent(self, sessions_dir):
        from mopsus.conversation import clear_session

        # Should not raise
        clear_session(99999)

    def test_atomic_write_creates_file(self, sessions_dir):
        from mopsus.conversation import set_session_id

        set_session_id(100, "sess-100")
        sessions_file = sessions_dir / "sessions.json"
        assert sessions_file.is_file()
        data = json.loads(sessions_file.read_text())
        assert data["100"]["session_id"] == "sess-100"

    def test_corrupted_file_returns_defaults(self, sessions_dir):
        from mopsus.conversation import get_session

        sessions_file = sessions_dir / "sessions.json"
        sessions_file.write_text("NOT VALID JSON{{{")
        s = get_session(12345)
        assert s["session_id"] is None
        assert s["model"] == "opus"

    def test_missing_file_returns_defaults(self, sessions_dir):
        from mopsus.conversation import get_session

        # sessions_dir exists but no file
        s = get_session(12345)
        assert s["session_id"] is None

    def test_multiple_chats_independent(self, sessions_dir):
        from mopsus.conversation import get_session, set_model, set_session_id

        set_session_id(111, "sess-a")
        set_model(111, "haiku")
        set_session_id(222, "sess-b")
        set_model(222, "sonnet")

        assert get_session(111)["session_id"] == "sess-a"
        assert get_session(111)["model"] == "haiku"
        assert get_session(222)["session_id"] == "sess-b"
        assert get_session(222)["model"] == "sonnet"

    def test_has_chat_state(self, sessions_dir):
        from mopsus.conversation import has_chat_state, set_session_id

        assert has_chat_state(12345) is False
        set_session_id(12345, "sess-1")
        assert has_chat_state(12345) is True


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# split_message tests
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


class TestSplitMessage:
    def test_short_no_split(self):
        from mopsus.agent import split_message

        assert split_message("hello") == ["hello"]

    def test_empty_string(self):
        from mopsus.agent import split_message

        assert split_message("") == [""]

    def test_multiline_split(self):
        from mopsus.agent import split_message

        # Create text that needs splitting
        lines = [f"line {i}: " + "x" * 50 for i in range(100)]
        text = "\n".join(lines)
        chunks = split_message(text, max_len=500)
        assert len(chunks) > 1
        # All chunks fit within limit
        for chunk in chunks:
            assert len(chunk) <= 500

    def test_single_very_long_line(self):
        from mopsus.agent import split_message

        line = "x" * 10000
        chunks = split_message(line, max_len=4096)
        assert len(chunks) > 1
        reconstructed = "".join(chunks)
        assert reconstructed == line

    def test_exact_limit(self):
        from mopsus.agent import split_message

        text = "x" * 4096
        assert split_message(text, max_len=4096) == [text]


class TestTelegramMarkdownRendering:
    def test_render_markdown_for_telegram_common_syntax(self):
        from mopsus.agent import render_markdown_for_telegram

        text = "## Title\n- item\n**bold** and `code` and [link](https://example.com)"
        rendered = render_markdown_for_telegram(text)
        assert "<b>Title</b>" in rendered
        assert "• item" in rendered
        assert "<b>bold</b>" in rendered
        assert "<code>code</code>" in rendered
        assert '<a href="https://example.com">link</a>' in rendered

    def test_render_markdown_for_telegram_code_fence(self):
        from mopsus.agent import render_markdown_for_telegram

        text = '```python\nprint("x")\n```'
        rendered = render_markdown_for_telegram(text)
        assert "<pre><code>" in rendered
        assert "print(&quot;x&quot;)" in rendered
        assert "```" not in rendered


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Auth guard tests
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


def _make_update(chat_id, user_id, chat_type=ChatType.PRIVATE):
    """Build a minimal Update-like object for auth testing."""
    update = SimpleNamespace()
    update.effective_chat = SimpleNamespace(id=chat_id, type=chat_type)
    update.effective_user = SimpleNamespace(id=user_id)
    return update


class TestAuthGuard:
    def test_authorized(self):
        from mopsus.agent import check_auth

        config = {"chat_id": 100, "user_id": 200}
        update = _make_update(100, 200)
        assert check_auth(update, config) is None

    def test_wrong_chat(self):
        from mopsus.agent import check_auth

        config = {"chat_id": 100, "user_id": 200}
        update = _make_update(999, 200)
        result = check_auth(update, config)
        assert result is not None
        assert "chat" in result.lower()

    def test_wrong_user(self):
        from mopsus.agent import check_auth

        config = {"chat_id": 100, "user_id": 200}
        update = _make_update(100, 999)
        result = check_auth(update, config)
        assert result is not None
        assert "user" in result.lower()

    def test_no_user_id_check(self):
        from mopsus.agent import check_auth

        config = {"chat_id": 100, "user_id": None}
        update = _make_update(100, 999)
        assert check_auth(update, config) is None

    def test_group_chat_rejected(self):
        from mopsus.agent import check_auth

        config = {"chat_id": 100, "user_id": None}
        update = _make_update(100, 200, chat_type=ChatType.GROUP)
        result = check_auth(update, config)
        assert result is not None
        assert "private" in result.lower()

    def test_no_chat(self):
        from mopsus.agent import check_auth

        config = {"chat_id": 100, "user_id": None}
        update = SimpleNamespace(effective_chat=None, effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=1))
        assert check_auth(update, config) is not None


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Env policy tests
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


class TestEnvPolicy:
    def test_build_subprocess_env_excludes_mopsus(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_subprocess_env

        fake_env = {
            "PATH": "/usr/bin",
            "HOME": "/Users/test",
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "secret",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "12345",
            "TELEGRAM_API_ID": "also-secret",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            env = build_subprocess_env()
            assert "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN" not in env
            assert "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID" not in env
            assert "TELEGRAM_API_ID" not in env
            assert env["PATH"] == "/usr/bin"
            assert env["HOME"] == "/Users/test"

    def test_build_subprocess_env_drops_claudecode(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_subprocess_env

        fake_env = {"PATH": "/usr/bin", "CLAUDECODE": "1"}
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            env = build_subprocess_env()
            assert "CLAUDECODE" not in env

    def test_build_subprocess_env_drops_claude_code_prefix(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_subprocess_env

        fake_env = {
            "PATH": "/usr/bin",
            "CLAUDE_CODE_SSE_PORT": "3000",
            "CLAUDE_CODE_ENTRYPOINT": "1",
            "CLAUDE_CONFIG_DIR": "/tmp/claude",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            env = build_subprocess_env()
            assert "CLAUDE_CODE_SSE_PORT" not in env
            assert "CLAUDE_CODE_ENTRYPOINT" not in env
            assert env.get("CLAUDE_CONFIG_DIR") == "/tmp/claude"


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Claude command building tests
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


class TestBuildClaudeCommand:
    def test_basic_command(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_claude_command

        config = {
            "permission_mode": "default",
            "allowed_tools": "Read,Glob,Grep",
            "allow_dangerous": False,
        }
        cmd = build_claude_command("sonnet", None, config)
        assert cmd[0] == "claude"
        assert "-p" in cmd
        assert "--output-format" in cmd
        assert "json" in cmd
        assert "--model" in cmd
        assert "sonnet" in cmd
        assert "--resume" not in cmd
        assert "--dangerously-skip-permissions" not in cmd
        # Message is passed via stdin, not as a positional arg
        assert "hello" not in cmd

    def test_prefers_configured_claude_bin(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_claude_command

        config = {
            "claude_bin": "/Users/v/.local/bin/claude",
            "permission_mode": "default",
            "allowed_tools": "Read,Glob,Grep",
            "allow_dangerous": False,
        }
        cmd = build_claude_command("opus", None, config)
        assert cmd[0] == "/Users/v/.local/bin/claude"

    def test_with_resume(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_claude_command

        config = {
            "permission_mode": "default",
            "allowed_tools": "Read,Glob",
            "allow_dangerous": False,
        }
        cmd = build_claude_command("opus", "sess-123", config)
        idx = cmd.index("--resume")
        assert cmd[idx + 1] == "sess-123"

    def test_dangerous_mode(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_claude_command

        config = {
            "permission_mode": "default",
            "allowed_tools": "Read",
            "allow_dangerous": True,
        }
        cmd = build_claude_command("opus", None, config)
        assert "--dangerously-skip-permissions" in cmd


class TestCodexHelpers:
    def test_parse_backend_request_defaults_to_claude(self):
        from mopsus.agent import parse_backend_request

        backend, prompt = parse_backend_request("hello there")
        assert backend == "claude"
        assert prompt == "hello there"

    def test_parse_backend_request_codex_colon(self):
        from mopsus.agent import parse_backend_request

        backend, prompt = parse_backend_request("codex: review this diff")
        assert backend == "codex"
        assert prompt == "review this diff"

    def test_parse_backend_request_codex_at_prefix(self):
        from mopsus.agent import parse_backend_request

        backend, prompt = parse_backend_request("@codex run tests")
        assert backend == "codex"
        assert prompt == "run tests"

    def test_build_codex_command(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_codex_command

        out = Path("/tmp/mopsus_codex_output.txt")
        cmd = build_codex_command(
            "hello", out, "gpt-5-codex", "workspace-write", "high"
        )
        assert cmd[:3] == ["codex", "exec", "--color"]
        assert "--model" in cmd
        model_idx = cmd.index("--model")
        assert cmd[model_idx + 1] == "gpt-5-codex"
        assert "--sandbox" in cmd
        sandbox_idx = cmd.index("--sandbox")
        assert cmd[sandbox_idx + 1] == "workspace-write"
        assert "-c" in cmd
        config_idx = cmd.index("-c")
        assert cmd[config_idx + 1] == 'model_reasoning_effort="high"'
        assert "--output-last-message" in cmd
        idx = cmd.index("--output-last-message")
        assert cmd[idx + 1] == str(out)
        assert cmd[-1] == "hello"

    def test_format_agent_header(self):
        from mopsus.agent import format_agent_header

        assert (
            format_agent_header("claude", "opus")
            == "[Mopsus Oracle | Claude opus]"
        )
        assert (
            format_agent_header("codex", "gpt-5-codex")
            == "[Patchsmith | Codex gpt-5-codex]"
        )


class TestSoulPrompt:
    def test_soul_prompt_included_in_command(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_claude_command

        config = {
            "permission_mode": "default",
            "allowed_tools": "Read,Glob",
            "allow_dangerous": False,
            "soul_prompt": "I am Mopsus, a wise oracle.",
        }
        cmd = build_claude_command("opus", None, config)
        idx = cmd.index("--append-system-prompt")
        assert cmd[idx + 1] == "I am Mopsus, a wise oracle."

    def test_soul_prompt_absent_when_empty(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_claude_command

        config = {
            "permission_mode": "default",
            "allowed_tools": "Read,Glob",
            "allow_dangerous": False,
            "soul_prompt": "",
        }
        cmd = build_claude_command("opus", None, config)
        assert "--append-system-prompt" not in cmd

    def test_soul_prompt_absent_when_missing(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_claude_command

        config = {
            "permission_mode": "default",
            "allowed_tools": "Read,Glob",
            "allow_dangerous": False,
        }
        cmd = build_claude_command("opus", None, config)
        assert "--append-system-prompt" not in cmd

    def test_get_config_loads_soul_file(self, tmp_path):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        soul_file = tmp_path / "soul.md"
        soul_file.write_text("I am the oracle.\n")
        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
        }
        with (
            patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True),
            patch("mopsus.agent.REPO_DIR", tmp_path),
        ):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["soul_prompt"] == "I am the oracle."

    def test_get_config_missing_soul_file(self, tmp_path):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
        }
        with (
            patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True),
            patch("mopsus.agent.REPO_DIR", tmp_path),
        ):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["soul_prompt"] == ""


class TestConfigAndModelSelection:
    def test_get_config_invalid_default_model_falls_back(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_DEFAULT_MODEL": "invalid-model",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["default_model"] == "opus"

    def test_get_config_sets_default_codex_model(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_model"] == "gpt-5-codex"
            assert config["codex_sandbox"] == "workspace-write"
            assert config["codex_reasoning_effort"] == "high"

    def test_get_config_prefers_configured_codex_bin(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_CODEX_BIN": "/Users/v/.bun/bin/codex",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_bin"] == "/Users/v/.bun/bin/codex"

    def test_get_config_prefers_configured_codex_sandbox(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_CODEX_SANDBOX": "read-only",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_sandbox"] == "read-only"

    def test_get_config_prefers_configured_codex_reasoning_effort(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_CODEX_REASONING_EFFORT": "medium",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_reasoning_effort"] == "medium"

    def test_get_config_loads_distinct_claude_and_codex_prompts(self, tmp_path):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        (tmp_path / "soul.md").write_text("Claude soul")
        (tmp_path / "situation.md").write_text("Claude situation")
        (tmp_path / "codex_soul.md").write_text("Codex soul")
        (tmp_path / "codex_situation.md").write_text("Codex situation")

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
        }
        with (
            patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True),
            patch("mopsus.agent.REPO_DIR", tmp_path),
        ):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["soul_prompt"] == "Claude soul\n\nClaude situation"
            assert config["codex_prompt"] == "Codex soul\n\nCodex situation"
            assert config["claude_prompt_files"] == ["soul.md", "situation.md"]
            assert config["codex_prompt_files"] == [
                "codex_soul.md",
                "codex_situation.md",
            ]

    def test_run_claude_uses_config_default_for_new_chat(self):
        from mopsus.agent import run_claude

        config = {"default_model": "sonnet", "allow_dangerous": False}

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent.get_session",
                    return_value={"session_id": None, "model": "opus"},
                ),
                patch("mopsus.agent.has_chat_state", return_value=False),
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent._run_claude_once",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("ok", "sess-new")),
                ) as mocked_run_once,
                patch("mopsus.agent.set_session_id") as mocked_set_session,
            ):
                response, session_id = await run_claude("hello", 123, config)
                mocked_run_once.assert_awaited_once_with(
                    "hello", "sonnet", None, config
                )
                mocked_set_session.assert_called_once_with(123, "sess-new")
                assert response == "ok"
                assert session_id == "sess-new"

        asyncio.run(_exercise())

    def test_voice_message_stub_is_reachable(self):
        from mopsus.agent import handle_message

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.text = None
                self.voice = object()
                self.audio = None
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(bot_data={"config": {}}, bot=SimpleNamespace())

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None):
                await handle_message(update, context)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert update.message.replies == ["Voice messages are not supported yet."]


class TestHelpCommand:
    def test_help_command_returns_usage(self):
        from mopsus.agent import cmd_help

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={"config": {"broadcast_mode": True, "chat_id": 100, "user_id": None}}
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None):
                await cmd_help(update, context)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert update.message.replies
        body = update.message.replies[0]
        assert "/help" in body
        assert "/status" in body
        assert "/codex <prompt>" in body
        assert "Broadcast mode: ON" in body

    def test_help_command_uses_effective_message(self):
        from mopsus.agent import cmd_help

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        effective_message = DummyMessage()
        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            effective_message=effective_message,
            message=None,
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={"config": {"broadcast_mode": True, "chat_id": 100, "user_id": None}}
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None):
                await cmd_help(update, context)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert effective_message.replies
        assert "Mopsus Help" in effective_message.replies[0]
        assert "Claude+Codex when broadcast is ON" in effective_message.replies[0]


class TestMessageRouting:
    def test_plain_text_broadcasts_to_both_backends(self):
        from mopsus.agent import handle_message

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.text = "hello team"
                self.voice = None
                self.audio = None
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={
                "config": {
                    "broadcast_mode": True,
                    "blackboard_enabled": False,
                    "chat_id": 100,
                    "user_id": None,
                }
            },
            bot=SimpleNamespace(),
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None),
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent._run_backend_request",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("ok", "model")),
                ) as mocked_backend,
            ):
                await handle_message(update, context)
                assert mocked_backend.await_count == 2
                called_backends = [
                    call.kwargs["backend"] for call in mocked_backend.await_args_list
                ]
                assert called_backends == ["claude", "codex"]

        asyncio.run(_exercise())

    def test_explicit_codex_stays_single_backend(self):
        from mopsus.agent import handle_message

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.text = "codex: quick check"
                self.voice = None
                self.audio = None
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={
                "config": {
                    "broadcast_mode": True,
                    "blackboard_enabled": False,
                    "chat_id": 100,
                    "user_id": None,
                }
            },
            bot=SimpleNamespace(),
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None),
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent._run_backend_request",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("ok", "model")),
                ) as mocked_backend,
            ):
                await handle_message(update, context)
                assert mocked_backend.await_count == 1
                assert mocked_backend.await_args_list[0].kwargs["backend"] == "codex"

        asyncio.run(_exercise())


class TestTypingLoop:
    def test_typing_loop_tolerates_timeout(self):
        from telegram.error import TimedOut

        from mopsus.agent import _typing_loop

        class DummyBot:
            def __init__(self):
                self.calls = 0

            async def send_chat_action(self, chat_id: int, action: str):
                self.calls += 1
                if self.calls == 1:
                    raise TimedOut("Timed out")
                raise asyncio.CancelledError

        bot = DummyBot()

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.asyncio.sleep", new=AsyncMock(return_value=None)):
                await _typing_loop(bot, 123)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert bot.calls == 2


class TestBackendAnnouncements:
    def test_codex_response_includes_speaker_header(self):
        from mopsus.agent import _run_backend_request

                self.placeholder = SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

                patch("mopsus.agent._typing_loop", new=AsyncMock(return_value=None)),

                    backend="codex",
                    prompt="do thing",
                    chat_id=123,

                    bot=bot,
                    config=config,

        assert sent.startswith("<b>[Patchsmith | Codex gpt-5-codex]</b>")

            def __init__(self):
                self.placeholder = SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                return self.placeholder

        message = DummyMessage()
        bot = SimpleNamespace(send_message=AsyncMock(), send_chat_action=AsyncMock())

            with (
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent.run_claude",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("All set.", None)),
                ),
                patch("mopsus.agent.has_chat_state", return_value=False),
                patch("mopsus.agent._typing_loop", new=AsyncMock(return_value=None)),

                    backend="claude",
                    prompt="do thing",
                    chat_id=123,
                    message=message,
                    bot=bot,
                    config=config,
                )

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        sent = message.placeholder.edit_text.await_args.args[0]
        assert sent.startswith("<b>[Mopsus Oracle | Claude sonnet]</b>")


Turn 1 - Assistant
Premise to challenge: “-100 LOC, zero behavior change” is the wrong target for this file. In [agent.py](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/tweets/mopsus/agent.py), reliability risk is concentrated in auth, routing, and queueing, not line count.

**RFC Revision (delta)**
- `#1 _env_choice`: **Implement now**. Low risk, real duplication removal.
- `#2 @authenticated decorator`: **Defer as proposed**. Decorator indirection on async Telegram handlers is harder to debug and can hide handler-specific edge cases.
- `#2 replacement`: **Implement now** as a plain helper (`_auth_and_message(update, context) -> tuple[config, message] | None`) to remove boilerplate without changing call style.
- `#3 _record_blackboard`: **Implement now**. Good dedupe if helper stays thin and side-effect free.
- `#4 delete parse_backend_request`: **Defer delete**. It is used by tests in [test_mopsus.py](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/tweets/tests/test_mopsus.py) and may be a soft API. Deprecate first, remove later.
- `#5 response formatting simplification`: **Implement now**.
- `#6 setdefault lock`: **Reject**. `setdefault(asyncio.Lock())` eagerly allocates a lock every call; tiny cost, but less explicit and no real reliability win.
- `#7 get_reply_message with or`: **Defer**. Keep explicit `is not None` semantics.
- `#8 return type annotation`: **Implement now** (independent of #7).
- `#9 remove redundant or ""`: **Defer**. Keep defensive normalization in a persistence-facing path.

**Implement-now slice (safe)**
- #1, #3, #5, #8, and helper-based replacement for #2.
- Expected effect: meaningful simplification with near-zero runtime risk.

**Reliability guardrails**
- Add regression tests before refactor: auth failure replies, `message is None` paths, blackboard append counts, queue “Queued” behavior.
- Keep behavior lockstep: no command output text changes in this round.
- Land in one PR with a rollback-friendly commit boundary (`helpers + no-op behavior tests` then `call-site rewrites`).

**Radical alternatives (risky, high payoff)**
- Kill implicit broadcast mode; require explicit `/both` or prefix. This removes dual-backend fanout complexity and blackboard race-like coupling.
- Replace per-chat lock with a per-chat actor task and inbox queue. Cleaner concurrency model, fewer handler conditionals.
- Split transport from orchestration: Telegram adapter becomes thin; a backend-agnostic turn engine handles auth, routing, context, and execution.

If you want, I can draft the exact PR plan as 3 commits with test cases mapped to each commit.

1. Remove implicit broadcast entirely; require explicit dual-run command to cut fanout/latency failure surface.
2. Replace JSON blackboard with SQLite WAL append log plus periodic compaction to avoid blocking rewrites.
3. Move handler logic into a pure “turn engine” function with contract tests; Telegram layer becomes thin I/O adapter only.
