        cmd = build_claude_command("opus", None, config)
        assert "--append-system-prompt" not in cmd

    def test_soul_prompt_absent_when_missing(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_claude_command

        config = {
            "permission_mode": "default",
            "allowed_tools": "Read,Glob",
            "allow_dangerous": False,
        }
        cmd = build_claude_command("opus", None, config)
        assert "--append-system-prompt" not in cmd

    def test_get_config_loads_soul_file(self, tmp_path):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        soul_file = tmp_path / "soul.md"
        soul_file.write_text("I am the oracle.\n")
        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
        }
        with (
            patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True),
            patch("mopsus.agent.REPO_DIR", tmp_path),
        ):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["soul_prompt"] == "I am the oracle."

    def test_get_config_missing_soul_file(self, tmp_path):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
        }
        with (
            patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True),
            patch("mopsus.agent.REPO_DIR", tmp_path),
        ):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["soul_prompt"] == ""


class TestConfigAndModelSelection:
    def test_get_config_invalid_default_model_falls_back(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_DEFAULT_MODEL": "invalid-model",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["default_model"] == "opus"

    def test_get_config_sets_default_codex_model(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_model"] == "gpt-5-codex"
            assert config["codex_sandbox"] == "workspace-write"
            assert config["codex_reasoning_effort"] == "high"

    def test_get_config_prefers_configured_codex_bin(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_CODEX_BIN": "/Users/v/.bun/bin/codex",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_bin"] == "/Users/v/.bun/bin/codex"

    def test_get_config_prefers_configured_codex_sandbox(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_CODEX_SANDBOX": "read-only",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_sandbox"] == "read-only"

    def test_get_config_prefers_configured_codex_reasoning_effort(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_CODEX_REASONING_EFFORT": "medium",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_reasoning_effort"] == "medium"

    def test_get_config_loads_distinct_claude_and_codex_prompts(self, tmp_path):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        (tmp_path / "soul.md").write_text("Claude soul")
        (tmp_path / "situation.md").write_text("Claude situation")
        (tmp_path / "codex_soul.md").write_text("Codex soul")
        (tmp_path / "codex_situation.md").write_text("Codex situation")

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
        }
        with (
            patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True),
            patch("mopsus.agent.REPO_DIR", tmp_path),
        ):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["soul_prompt"] == "Claude soul\n\nClaude situation"
            assert config["codex_prompt"] == "Codex soul\n\nCodex situation"
            assert config["claude_prompt_files"] == ["soul.md", "situation.md"]
            assert config["codex_prompt_files"] == [
                "codex_soul.md",
                "codex_situation.md",
            ]

    def test_run_claude_uses_config_default_for_new_chat(self):
        from mopsus.agent import run_claude

        config = {"default_model": "sonnet", "allow_dangerous": False}

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent.get_session",
                    return_value={"session_id": None, "model": "opus"},
                ),
                patch("mopsus.agent.has_chat_state", return_value=False),
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent._run_claude_once",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("ok", "sess-new")),
                ) as mocked_run_once,
                patch("mopsus.agent.set_session_id") as mocked_set_session,
            ):
                response, session_id = await run_claude("hello", 123, config)
                mocked_run_once.assert_awaited_once_with(
                    "hello", "sonnet", None, config
                )
                mocked_set_session.assert_called_once_with(123, "sess-new")
                assert response == "ok"
                assert session_id == "sess-new"

        asyncio.run(_exercise())

    def test_voice_message_stub_is_reachable(self):
        from mopsus.agent import handle_message

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.text = None
                self.voice = object()
                self.audio = None
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(bot_data={"config": {}}, bot=SimpleNamespace())

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None):
                await handle_message(update, context)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert update.message.replies == ["Voice messages are not supported yet."]


class TestHelpCommand:
    def test_help_command_returns_usage(self):
        from mopsus.agent import cmd_help

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={"config": {"broadcast_mode": True, "chat_id": 100, "user_id": None}}
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None):
                await cmd_help(update, context)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert update.message.replies
        body = update.message.replies[0]
        assert "/help" in body
        assert "/status" in body
        assert "/codex <prompt>" in body
        assert "Broadcast mode: ON" in body

    def test_help_command_uses_effective_message(self):
        from mopsus.agent import cmd_help

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        effective_message = DummyMessage()
        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            effective_message=effective_message,
            message=None,
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={"config": {"broadcast_mode": True, "chat_id": 100, "user_id": None}}
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None):
                await cmd_help(update, context)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert effective_message.replies
        assert "Mopsus Help" in effective_message.replies[0]
        assert "Claude+Codex when broadcast is ON" in effective_message.replies[0]


class TestMessageRouting:
    def test_plain_text_broadcasts_to_both_backends(self):
        from mopsus.agent import handle_message

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.text = "hello team"
                self.voice = None
                self.audio = None
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={
                "config": {
                    "broadcast_mode": True,
                    "blackboard_enabled": False,
                    "chat_id": 100,
                    "user_id": None,
                }
            },
            bot=SimpleNamespace(),
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None),
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent._run_backend_request",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("ok", "model")),
                ) as mocked_backend,
            ):
                await handle_message(update, context)
                assert mocked_backend.await_count == 2
                called_backends = [
                    call.kwargs["backend"] for call in mocked_backend.await_args_list
                ]
                assert called_backends == ["claude", "codex"]

        asyncio.run(_exercise())

    def test_explicit_codex_stays_single_backend(self):
        from mopsus.agent import handle_message

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.text = "codex: quick check"
                self.voice = None
                self.audio = None
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={
                "config": {
                    "broadcast_mode": True,
                    "blackboard_enabled": False,
                    "chat_id": 100,
                    "user_id": None,
                }
            },
            bot=SimpleNamespace(),
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None),
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent._run_backend_request",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("ok", "model")),
                ) as mocked_backend,
            ):
                await handle_message(update, context)
                assert mocked_backend.await_count == 1
                assert mocked_backend.await_args_list[0].kwargs["backend"] == "codex"

        asyncio.run(_exercise())


class TestTypingLoop:
    def test_typing_loop_tolerates_timeout(self):
        from telegram.error import TimedOut

        from mopsus.agent import _typing_loop

        class DummyBot:
            def __init__(self):
                self.calls = 0

            async def send_chat_action(self, chat_id: int, action: str):
                self.calls += 1
                if self.calls == 1:
                    raise TimedOut("Timed out")
                raise asyncio.CancelledError

        bot = DummyBot()

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.asyncio.sleep", new=AsyncMock(return_value=None)):
                await _typing_loop(bot, 123)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert bot.calls == 2


class TestBackendAnnouncements:
    def test_codex_response_includes_speaker_header(self):
        from mopsus.agent import _run_backend_request

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.placeholder = SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                return self.placeholder

        message = DummyMessage()
        bot = SimpleNamespace(send_message=AsyncMock(), send_chat_action=AsyncMock())
        config = {"default_model": "opus", "codex_model": "gpt-5-codex"}

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent.run_codex", new=AsyncMock(return_value="Implemented.")
                ),
                patch("mopsus.agent._typing_loop", new=AsyncMock(return_value=None)),
            ):
                await _run_backend_request(
                    backend="codex",
                    prompt="do thing",
                    chat_id=123,
                    message=message,
                    bot=bot,
                    config=config,
                )

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        sent = message.placeholder.edit_text.await_args.args[0]
        assert sent.startswith("<b>[Patchsmith | Codex gpt-5-codex]</b>")

    def test_claude_response_includes_speaker_header(self):
        from mopsus.agent import _run_backend_request

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.placeholder = SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                return self.placeholder

        message = DummyMessage()
        bot = SimpleNamespace(send_message=AsyncMock(), send_chat_action=AsyncMock())
        config = {"default_model": "sonnet", "codex_model": "gpt-5-codex"}

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent.run_claude",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("All set.", None)),
                ),
                patch("mopsus.agent.has_chat_state", return_value=False),
                patch("mopsus.agent._typing_loop", new=AsyncMock(return_value=None)),
            ):
                await _run_backend_request(
                    backend="claude",
                    prompt="do thing",
                    chat_id=123,
                    message=message,
                    bot=bot,
                    config=config,
                )

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        sent = message.placeholder.edit_text.await_args.args[0]
        assert sent.startswith("<b>[Mopsus Oracle | Claude sonnet]</b>")


Here is the first proposal:

Premise to challenge: “-100 LOC, zero behavior change” is the wrong target for this file. In [agent.py](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/tweets/mopsus/agent.py), reliability risk is concentrated in auth, routing, and queueing, not line count.

**RFC Revision (delta)**
- `#1 _env_choice`: **Implement now**. Low risk, real duplication removal.
- `#2 @authenticated decorator`: **Defer as proposed**. Decorator indirection on async Telegram handlers is harder to debug and can hide handler-specific edge cases.
- `#2 replacement`: **Implement now** as a plain helper (`_auth_and_message(update, context) -> tuple[config, message] | None`) to remove boilerplate without changing call style.
- `#3 _record_blackboard`: **Implement now**. Good dedupe if helper stays thin and side-effect free.
- `#4 delete parse_backend_request`: **Defer delete**. It is used by tests in [test_mopsus.py](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/tweets/tests/test_mopsus.py) and may be a soft API. Deprecate first, remove later.
- `#5 response formatting simplification`: **Implement now**.
- `#6 setdefault lock`: **Reject**. `setdefault(asyncio.Lock())` eagerly allocates a lock every call; tiny cost, but less explicit and no real reliability win.
- `#7 get_reply_message with or`: **Defer**. Keep explicit `is not None` semantics.
- `#8 return type annotation`: **Implement now** (independent of #7).
- `#9 remove redundant or ""`: **Defer**. Keep defensive normalization in a persistence-facing path.

**Implement-now slice (safe)**
- #1, #3, #5, #8, and helper-based replacement for #2.
- Expected effect: meaningful simplification with near-zero runtime risk.

**Reliability guardrails**
- Add regression tests before refactor: auth failure replies, `message is None` paths, blackboard append counts, queue “Queued” behavior.
- Keep behavior lockstep: no command output text changes in this round.
- Land in one PR with a rollback-friendly commit boundary (`helpers + no-op behavior tests` then `call-site rewrites`).

**Radical alternatives (risky, high payoff)**
- Kill implicit broadcast mode; require explicit `/both` or prefix. This removes dual-backend fanout complexity and blackboard race-like coupling.
- Replace per-chat lock with a per-chat actor task and inbox queue. Cleaner concurrency model, fewer handler conditionals.
- Split transport from orchestration: Telegram adapter becomes thin; a backend-agnostic turn engine handles auth, routing, context, and execution.

If you want, I can draft the exact PR plan as 3 commits with test cases mapped to each commit.

Turn 1 - Assistant
**Findings**
1. High: your `#2` helper shape can silently change behavior for `/reset`. In current code, state is cleared even if `message` is `None`; a combined `_auth_and_message(...)->None` gate risks skipping reset entirely. See [agent.py#L872](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/tweets/mopsus/agent.py#L872).
2. Medium: `#3` helper must preserve one-time `max_entries` evaluation per turn, not recompute from mutable config at each append, or you can get asymmetric user/assistant retention. See [agent.py#L1150](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/tweets/mopsus/agent.py#L1150).
3. Medium: `#4` “defer delete” is right, but “tests use it” is weak policy. If it’s internal, migrate tests now and keep a temporary compatibility shim with explicit removal date. See [agent.py#L598](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/tweets/mopsus/agent.py#L598) and [test_mopsus.py](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/tweets/tests/test_mopsus.py).
4. Medium: reliability guardrails are incomplete; queue tests must be concurrent (two overlapping requests) to validate lock/user-visible “Queued” semantics, not just single-call paths. See [agent.py#L845](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/tweets/mopsus/agent.py#L845).

**Revision Delta**
```diff
- #2 replacement: Implement now as _auth_and_message(update, context) -> tuple[config, message] | None
+ #2 replacement: Implement now as _auth_guard(update, config, message) -> bool
+ Keep message-null handling per handler to avoid /reset regression.

- #3 _record_blackboard: helper reads config each call
+ #3 _record_blackboard: pass max_entries explicitly from caller (computed once per turn).

- #4 defer delete because tests use parse_backend_request
+ #4 keep wrapper with deprecation comment + target removal date; migrate tests to parse_backend_request_details now.
```

**Implement Now**
1. `#1`, `#3` (with explicit `max_entries` arg), `#5`, `#8`, and `_auth_guard` (not `_auth_and_message`).

**Defer**
1. Decorator form of `#2`, delete of `#4`, `#6`, `#7`, `#9`.

**Radical (risky, high-payoff)**
1. Remove implicit broadcast entirely; require explicit dual-run command to cut fanout/latency failure surface.
2. Replace JSON blackboard with SQLite WAL append log plus periodic compaction to avoid blocking rewrites.
3. Move handler logic into a pure “turn engine” function with contract tests; Telegram layer becomes thin I/O adapter only.

Turn 2 - User
[Creativity: 4/5] Suggest improvements and alternatives. Challenge assumptions. Consider non-obvious solutions.

Your revision delta is correct. I’d proceed with this tighter plan.

**Implement Now**
1. `#1` `_env_choice` in `get_config()`.
2. `#3` `_record_blackboard(...)` but pass `max_entries` from caller (computed once per turn).
3. `#5` simplify `_run_backend_request` response-body derivation.
4. `#8` add `get_reply_message(...) -> Message | None`.
5. Replace duplicated auth preamble with `_auth_guard(update, config, message) -> bool`; keep per-handler `message is None` handling so `/reset` still clears state even without a replyable message.

**Defer**
1. Decorator form of `#2`.
2. Hard delete of `parse_backend_request`; keep shim + deprecation note and migrate tests first.
3. `#6` `setdefault` lock change.
4. `#7` `or`-based `get_reply_message`.
5. `#9` removing defensive `or ""` in blackboard cleaner.

**Reliability Gates (must add before refactor)**
1. `/reset` clears session/blackboard when `message is None` ([agent.py](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/tweets/mopsus/agent.py)).
2. Concurrent queue test with two overlapping requests verifies exactly one “Queued” and strict serialization.
3. Blackboard append symmetry test: one user append + one assistant append per backend in a turn.
4. Compatibility test for `parse_backend_request` shim while new tests use `parse_backend_request_details`.

**Non-obvious high-payoff next step**
1. Add `MOPSUS_BROADCAST_MODE=explicit` experiment: no implicit dual-run; require `/both` or prefix. This cuts latency, token burn, and failure surface more than any LOC refactor.

If you want, I can draft the exact 3-commit sequence and test names next.

Turn 3 - User
[Creativity: 3/5] Mix new ideas with refinement. Address open questions. Weigh tradeoffs.

This sequence is strong and I’d run it with a few refinements to reduce false confidence.

**Refined commit map**

1. **Commit 1: tests only**
- Keep your 4 new tests.
- Make the queue test deterministic: gate the first `_run_backend_request` with an `asyncio.Event`, start a second `handle_message`, assert one `"Queued — waiting for current request to finish."`, then release and assert call order.
- In blackboard symmetry, assert exact append tuples per turn (`user` once, `assistant` once per backend actually run), and cover broadcast ON/OFF + explicit prefix.
- Migrate parser tests to `parse_backend_request_details` as primary, keep one shim-compat test for `parse_backend_request`.

2. **Commit 2: auth/config**
- Implement `_env_choice` and apply to default model, codex sandbox, reasoning effort.
- Add `Message` import and `get_reply_message(update: Update) -> Message | None` without changing explicit semantics.
- Implement `_auth_guard(update, config, message) -> bool` (returns `True` when request handled/blocked).
- Keep per-handler `message is None` handling, especially `/reset`, so state clear still executes.

3. **Commit 3: blackboard + response cleanup**
- Add `_record_blackboard(..., max_entries: int)` and pass `max_entries` computed once per turn from callers.
- Apply `_run_backend_request` simplification:
  - `raw_response = response_text or ""`
  - `response_body = raw_response.lstrip("\r\n")`
- Keep `parse_backend_request` wrapper with a deprecation comment and concrete removal target date.

**Open policy choice to lock now**
- Set a specific shim removal date in code/docs (for example, `2026-06-30`) so deferment doesn’t become permanent.

Turn 3 - Assistant
Lock the shim policy now: keep `parse_backend_request` with a deprecation comment and target removal date `2026-06-30`, but do not emit `warnings.warn()` yet (avoids noisy runtime behavior changes).

**Exact test scaffolding** (add in [tweets/tests/test_mopsus.py](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/tweets/tests/test_mopsus.py)):

1. `test_cmd_reset_clears_state_when_message_none`
- Build `update` with valid `effective_chat/effective_user`, `message=None`, `effective_message=None`.
- Patch `check_auth -> None`, `clear_session`, `clear_blackboard`.
- Call `cmd_reset(update, context)`.
- Assert `clear_session(chat_id)` and `clear_blackboard(chat_id)` were each called once.

2. `test_handle_message_concurrent_requests_queue_once_and_serialize`
- Use `broadcast_mode=False`, `blackboard_enabled=False`.
- Patch `_run_backend_request` with an `async` side effect:
  - First call sets `entered_first` event and blocks on `release_first`.
  - Second call only proceeds after first releases.
  - Record `order.append(("start"/"end", prompt))`.
- Start first `handle_message` task, wait for `entered_first`.
- Start second `handle_message` task, yield once.
- Assert second message got exactly one reply: `"Queued — waiting for current request to finish."`
- Release first, await both tasks.
- Assert strict order: first start/end completes before second start.

3. `test_blackboard_append_symmetry_per_backend_turn`
- Parametrize cases:
  - Plain text + `broadcast_mode=True` -> expected assistant backends `["claude","codex"]`.
  - Plain text + `broadcast_mode=False` -> `["claude"]`.
  - `"codex: ..."` + `broadcast_mode=True` -> `["codex"]`.
- Patch `append_blackboard_entry` and `_run_backend_request`.
- Call `handle_message`.
- Assert exactly one user append (`role="user", backend="user"`) and one assistant append per actual backend, in order.

4. `test_parse_backend_request_shim_compatible_with_details`
- For sample inputs (`"hello"`, `"codex: x"`, `"@codex x"`, `"claude x"`):
  - Compare `(backend, prompt)` from `parse_backend_request(...)`
  - Against first two values from `parse_backend_request_details(...)`.
- Keep this as the only shim-focused test; migrate parser behavior tests to `parse_backend_request_details`.

Turn 4 - User

Locked.

1. Shim policy:

- Add deprecation comment only, no `warnings.warn()` yet.
- Use this exact target in code: `Target removal date: 2026-06-30`.

1. Replace parser-behavior tests in `TestCodexHelpers` to target `parse_backend_request_details`:

```python
class TestCodexHelpers:
    def test_parse_backend_request_details_defaults_to_claude(self):
        from mopsus.agent import parse_backend_request_details

        backend, prompt, explicit_backend = parse_backend_request_details("hello there")
        assert backend == "claude"
        assert prompt == "hello there"
        assert explicit_backend is False

    def test_parse_backend_request_details_codex_colon(self):
        from mopsus.agent import parse_backend_request_details

        backend, prompt, explicit_backend = parse_backend_request_details("codex: review this diff")
        assert backend == "codex"
        assert prompt == "review this diff"
        assert explicit_backend is True

    def test_parse_backend_request_details_codex_at_prefix(self):
        from mopsus.agent import parse_backend_request_details

        backend, prompt, explicit_backend = parse_backend_request_details("@codex run tests")
        assert backend == "codex"
        assert prompt == "run tests"
        assert explicit_backend is True

    def test_parse_backend_request_details_claude_prefix(self):
        from mopsus.agent import parse_backend_request_details

        backend, prompt, explicit_backend = parse_backend_request_details("claude x")
        assert backend == "claude"
        assert prompt == "x"
        assert explicit_backend is True
```

2. Add shim compatibility test (only shim-focused test):

```python
    def test_parse_backend_request_shim_compatible_with_details(self):
        from mopsus.agent import parse_backend_request, parse_backend_request_details

        for sample in ("hello", "codex: x", "@codex x", "claude x"):
            backend, prompt = parse_backend_request(sample)
            details_backend, details_prompt, _ = parse_backend_request_details(sample)
            assert (backend, prompt) == (details_backend, details_prompt)
```

class TestResetCommand:
    def test_cmd_reset_clears_state_when_message_none(self):
        from mopsus.agent import cmd_reset

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=None,
            effective_message=None,
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(bot_data={"config": {"chat_id": 100, "user_id": None}})

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None),
                patch("mopsus.agent.clear_session") as mocked_clear_session,
                patch("mopsus.agent.clear_blackboard") as mocked_clear_blackboard,
            ):

4. Add concurrent queue serialization test to `TestMessageRouting`:

```python
    def test_handle_message_concurrent_requests_queue_once_and_serialize(self):
        from mopsus import agent
        from mopsus.agent import handle_message

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self, text: str):
                self.text = text
                self.voice = None
                self.audio = None
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update1 = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage("first prompt"),
        )
        update2 = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage("second prompt"),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={
                "config": {
                    "broadcast_mode": False,
                    "blackboard_enabled": False,
                    "chat_id": 100,
                    "user_id": None,
                }
            },
            bot=SimpleNamespace(),
        )

        entered_first = asyncio.Event()
        release_first = asyncio.Event()
        order: list[tuple[str, str]] = []
        first_call = True

        async def backend_side_effect(*, prompt: str, **kwargs):
            nonlocal first_call
            if first_call:
                first_call = False
                order.append(("start", prompt))
                entered_first.set()
                await release_first.wait()
                order.append(("end", prompt))
                return ("ok", "model")
            order.append(("start", prompt))
            order.append(("end", prompt))
            return ("ok", "model")

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None),
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent._run_backend_request",
                    new=AsyncMock(side_effect=backend_side_effect),
                ),
            ):
                task1 = asyncio.create_task(handle_message(update1, context))
                await entered_first.wait()
                task2 = asyncio.create_task(handle_message(update2, context))
                await asyncio.sleep(0)
                assert update2.message.replies == ["Queued — waiting for current request to finish."]
                release_first.set()
                await asyncio.gather(task1, task2)

        agent._chat_locks.clear()
        try:
            asyncio.run(_exercise())
        finally:
            agent._chat_locks.clear()

        assert order == [
            ("start", "first prompt"),
            ("end", "first prompt"),
            ("start", "second prompt"),
            ("end", "second prompt"),
        ]
```

5. Add blackboard symmetry test to `TestMessageRouting`:

```python
    @pytest.mark.parametrize(
        ("text", "broadcast_mode", "expected_assistant_backends"),
        [
            ("hello team", True, ["claude", "codex"]),
            ("hello team", False, ["claude"]),
            ("codex: quick check", True, ["codex"]),
        ],
    )
    def test_blackboard_append_symmetry_per_backend_turn(
        self,
        text: str,
        broadcast_mode: bool,
        expected_assistant_backends: list[str],
    ):
        from mopsus.agent import handle_message

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self, body: str):
                self.text = body
                self.voice = None
                self.audio = None
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(text),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={
                "config": {
                    "broadcast_mode": broadcast_mode,
                    "blackboard_enabled": True,
                    "chat_id": 100,
                    "user_id": None,
                }
            },
            bot=SimpleNamespace(),
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None),
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent._run_backend_request",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("ok", "model")),
                ),
                patch("mopsus.agent.append_blackboard_entry") as mocked_append,
            ):
                await handle_message(update, context)
                return mocked_append.call_args_list

        calls = asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert len(calls) == 1 + len(expected_assistant_backends)
        assert calls[0].kwargs["role"] == "user"
        assert calls[0].kwargs["backend"] == "user"
        assistants = calls[1:]
        assert [call.kwargs["backend"] for call in assistants] == expected_assistant_backends
        assert all(call.kwargs["role"] == "assistant" for call in assistants)
```

2. Add `_env_choice` near `_env_bool`:
```python
def _env_choice(name: str, valid: set[str], default: str, *, lower: bool = True) -> str:
    """Read an env var, validate against choices, warn, and fall back."""
    raw = os.environ.get(name, default).strip()
    if lower:
        raw = raw.lower()
    if raw in valid:
        return raw
    log.warning("Invalid %s=%r; falling back to %r", name, raw, default)
    return default
```

3. In `get_config()`, replace model/sandbox/reasoning parsing with:
```python
default_model = _env_choice("MOPSUS_DEFAULT_MODEL", VALID_MODELS, "opus")
codex_model = os.environ.get("MOPSUS_CODEX_MODEL", DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL).strip()
if not codex_model:
    codex_model = DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL
codex_sandbox = _env_choice(
    "MOPSUS_CODEX_SANDBOX",
    {"read-only", "workspace-write", "danger-full-access"},
    "workspace-write",
    lower=False,
)
codex_reasoning_effort = _env_choice(
    "MOPSUS_CODEX_REASONING_EFFORT",
    {"low", "medium", "high"},
    "high",
)
```

5. Add `_auth_guard`:
```python
async def _auth_guard(update: Update, config: dict, message: Message | None) -> bool:
    """Return True when auth fails and the request is handled."""
    if (err := check_auth(update, config)):
        if message is not None:
            await message.reply_text(err)
        return True
    return False
```

    return

**Commit 3 (`blackboard/response cleanup`)**  
Edit [agent.py](/Users/v/Code%202026/tweets/mopsus/agent.py).

1. Add `_record_blackboard` helper:
```python
def _record_blackboard(
    chat_id: int,
    *,
    role: str,
    backend: str,
    text: str,
    config: dict,
    max_entries: int,
    model: str | None = None,
) -> None:
    """Append a blackboard entry if blackboard recording is enabled."""
    if not config.get("blackboard_enabled", True):
        return
    append_blackboard_entry(
        chat_id,
        role=role,
        backend=backend,
        model=model,
        text=text,
        max_entries=max_entries,
    )
```

```

# Deprecated compatibility wrapper.
# Target removal date: 2026-06-30.
def parse_backend_request(text: str) -> tuple[str, str]:
    """Return (backend, prompt) for a user message.

    Prefer parse_backend_request_details for new call sites.
    """
    backend, prompt, _ = parse_backend_request_details(text)
    return backend, prompt
```
